\DoxyCodeLine{00954\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ 1\ }\textcolor{comment}{//\ parser\ helper\ macros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00955\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00956\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Q:\ "{}what\ the\ fuck\ is\ this?\ MACROS????"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00957\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A:\ The\ parser\ needs\ to\ work\ in\ exceptionless\ mode\ (returning\ error\ objects\ directly)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00958\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ and\ exception\ mode\ (reporting\ parse\ failures\ by\ throwing).\ Two\ totally\ different\ control\ flows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00959\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ These\ macros\ encapsulate\ the\ differences\ between\ the\ two\ modes\ so\ I\ can\ write\ code\ code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00960\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ as\ though\ I\ was\ only\ targeting\ one\ mode\ and\ not\ want\ yeet\ myself\ into\ the\ sun.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00961\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ They're\ all\ \#undef'd\ at\ the\ bottom\ of\ the\ parser's\ implementation\ so\ they\ should\ be\ harmless\ outside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00962\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ of\ toml++.}}
